**lib/internal/modules/esm/create_dynamic_module.js** handles dynamic module creation with:\\n- `createDynamicModule()`: Creates modules with specified imports/exports programmatically\\n- Used for WebAssembly, JSON, and synthetic modules\\n\\n## Module Caching\\nThe **lib/internal/modules/esm/module_map.js** implements caching:\\n- `ResolveCache`: Caches resolution results (specifier, parentURL, importAttributes) → (url, format)\\n- `LoadCache`: Caches loaded modules by URL\\n- Uses serialized keys for consistent cache lookups\\n\\n## Import Meta Handling\\nThe **lib/internal/modules/esm/initialize_import_meta.js** initializes import.meta:\\n- `initializeImportMeta()` (line 56): Sets url, dirname, filename for file: URLs\\n- `createImportMetaResolve()`: Provides import.meta.resolve() for synchronous specifier resolution\\n\\n## Module Loading\\nThe **lib/internal/modules/esm/load.js** implements the default loader:\\n- `getSource()`: Loads module source from file:, data:, or other protocols\\n- `getSourceSync()`: Synchronous variant for require() in imported CJS\\n- Handles reading files, data URLs, and validates URLs\\n\\n## Assertion and Import Attributes\\nThe **lib/internal/modules/esm/assert.js** validates import attributes:\\n- Validates import assertions (with syntax)\\n- Maps formats to allowed attribute types\\n- Handles Node.js-specific functionality\\n- Methods for module instantiation, evaluation, and namespace access\\n- Linking dependencies via `link()` method\\n- Handles synthetic evaluation steps for dynamic modules\\n- Module status tracking and hash-based lookup\\n- Integration with V8's module system\\n\\n## Utilities\\nThe **lib/internal/modules/esm/utils.js** provides:\\n- `compileSourceTextModule()` (line 336): Creates ModuleWrap from source text\\n- `getTranslators()`: Lazy-loads translators\\n- `registerModule()`: Registers modules for import.meta and dynamic import handling\\n- `initializeESM()`: Initializes the ESM loader infrastructure\\n- `initializeHooks()`: Sets up custom loader hooks\\n- `getDefaultConditions()`: Gets default resolution conditions\\n\\n## Resolution Flow\\n1. **Entry point detection**: `executeUserEntryPoint()` → `shouldUseESMLoader()`\\n2. **Module request**: `import` statement or `import()` expression\\n3. **Resolution**: `ModuleLoader.resolve()` → `resolveESM()` in resolve.js\\n4. **Loading**: `ModuleLoader.load()` → reads source → detects format\\n5. **Translation**: Format-specific translator creates ModuleWrap\\n6. **Job creation**: `ModuleLoader.getModuleJobForImport()` → `ModuleJob` instance\\n7. **Linking**: `ModuleJob._link()` → recursively loads and links dependencies\\n8. **Instantiation**: `ModuleJob._instantiate()` → `module.instantiate()`\\n9. **Evaluation**: `ModuleJob.run()` → `module.evaluate()`\\n\\n## CJS Fallback for Ambiguous Files\\nWhen a .js file has no package.json type field:\\n1. First attempt CommonJS loading\\n2. If imports ESM syntax, retry with ESM\\n3. Uses content detection in `get_format.js`\\n4.
